<pr_description>
TypeError: Body is unusable
### What version of Hono are you using?

4.8.3

### What runtime/platform is your app running on? (with version if possible)

Node

### What steps can reproduce the bug?

Add 2x `zValidators` for path/middleware for json, header and try to access raw body text in route handler.

From my investigations, [this](https://github.com/honojs/hono/blob/main/src/validator/validator.ts#L78) is causing the error. If we clone the json using `await c.req.raw.clone().json()`, it works fine.

Example using create hono app:
```
import { serve } from "@hono/node-server";
import { Hono } from "hono";
import { z } from "zod";
import { zValidator } from "@hono/zod-validator";

const schema = z.object({  mock: z.string() });

const app = new Hono();

app
  .get("/", (c) => {
    return c.text("Hello Hono!");
  })
  .post(
    "/",
    zValidator("header", schema),
    zValidator("json", schema),
    async (c) => {
      // causes error
      console.log(await c.req.raw.clone().text());

      return c.text("Hello Hono!");
    }
  );

serve(
  {
    fetch: app.fetch,
    port: 3000,
  },
  (info) => {
    console.log(`Server is running on http://localhost:${info.port}`);
  }
);
```

### What is the expected behavior?

I'm able to use multiple zValidators - especially for json & header - and still access the raw body.

### What do you see instead?


     6	import { bufferToFormData } from '../utils/buffer'
     7	
     8	type ValidationTargetKeysWithBody = 'form' | 'json'
     9	type ValidationTargetByMethod<M> = M extends 'get' | 'head' // GET and HEAD request must not have a body content.
    10	  ? Exclude<keyof ValidationTargets, ValidationTargetKeysWithBody>
    11	  : keyof ValidationTargets
    12	
    13	export type ValidationFunction<
    14	  InputType,
    15	  OutputType,
    16	  E extends Env = {},
    17	  P extends string = string
    18	> = (
    19	  value: InputType,
    20	  c: Context<E, P>
    21	) => OutputType | Response | Promise<OutputType> | Promise<Response>
    22	
    23	// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
    24	type ExcludeResponseType<T> = T extends Response & TypedResponse<any> ? never : T
    25	
    26	const jsonRegex = /^application\/([a-z-\.]+\+)?json(;\s*[a-zA-Z0-9\-]+\=([^;]+))*$/
    27	const multipartRegex = /^multipart\/form-data(;\s?boundary=[a-zA-Z0-9'"()+_,\-./:=?]+)?$/
    28	const urlencodedRegex = /^application\/x-www-form-urlencoded(;\s*[a-zA-Z0-9\-]+\=([^;]+))*$/
    29	
    30	export const validator = <
    31	  InputType,
    32	  P extends string,
    33	  M extends string,
    34	  U extends ValidationTargetByMethod<M>,
    35	  OutputType = ValidationTargets[U],
    36	  OutputTypeExcludeResponseType = ExcludeResponseType<OutputType>,
    37	  P2 extends string = P,
    38	  V extends {
    39	    in: {
    40	      [K in U]: K extends 'json'
    41	        ? unknown extends InputType
    42	          ? OutputTypeExcludeResponseType
    43	          : InputType
    44	        : { [K2 in keyof OutputTypeExcludeResponseType]: ValidationTargets[K][K2] }
    45	    }
    46	    out: { [K in U]: OutputTypeExcludeResponseType }
    47	  } = {
    48	    in: {
    49	      [K in U]: K extends 'json'
    50	        ? unknown extends InputType
    51	          ? OutputTypeExcludeResponseType
    52	          : InputType
    53	        : { [K2 in keyof OutputTypeExcludeResponseType]: ValidationTargets[K][K2] }
    54	    }
    55	    out: { [K in U]: OutputTypeExcludeResponseType }
    56	  },
    57	  // eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any
    58	  E extends Env = any
    59	>(
    60	  target: U,
    61	  validationFunc: ValidationFunction<
    62	    unknown extends InputType ? ValidationTargets[U] : InputType,
    63	    OutputType,
    64	    E,
    65	    P2
    66	  >
    67	): MiddlewareHandler<E, P, V> => {
    68	  return async (c, next) => {
    69	    let value = {}
    70	    const contentType = c.req.header('Content-Type')
    71	
    72	    switch (target) {
    73	      case 'json':
    74	        if (!contentType || !jsonRegex.test(contentType)) {
    75	          break
    76	        }
    77	        try {
    78	          value = await c.req.json()
    79	        } catch {
    80	          const message = 'Malformed JSON in request body'
    81	          throw new HTTPException(400, { message })
    82	        }
    83	        break
    84	      case 'form': {
    85	        if (
    86	          !contentType ||
    87	          !(multipartRegex.test(contentType) || urlencodedRegex.test(contentType))
    88	        ) {
    89	          break
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        let formData: FormData
    93	
    94	        if (c.req.bodyCache.formData) {
    95	          formData = await c.req.bodyCache.formData
    96	        } else {
    97	          try {
    98	            const arrayBuffer = await c.req.arrayBuffer()
    99	            formData = await bufferToFormData(arrayBuffer, contentType)
   100	            c.req.bodyCache.formData = formData
   101	          } catch (e) {
   102	            let message = 'Malformed FormData request.'
   103	            message += e instanceof Error ? ` ${e.message}` : ` ${String(e)}`
   104	            throw new HTTPException(400, { message })
   105	          }
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        const form: BodyData<{ all: true }> = {}
   109	        formData.forEach((value, key) => {
   110	          if (key.endsWith('[]')) {
   111	            ;((form[key] ??= []) as unknown[]).push(value)
   112	          } else if (Array.isArray(form[key])) {
   113	            ;(form[key] as unknown[]).push(value)
   114	          } else if (key in form) {
   115	            form[key] = [form[key] as string | File, value]
   116	          } else {
   117	            form[key] = value
   118	          }
   119	        })
   120	        value = form
   121	        break
   122	      }
   123	      case 'query':
   124	        value = Object.fromEntries(
   125	          Object.entries(c.req.queries()).map(([k, v]) => {
   126	            return v.length === 1 ? [k, v[0]] : [k, v]
   127	          })
   128	        )
   129	        break
   130	      case 'param':
   131	        value = c.req.param() as Record<string, string>
   132	        break
   133	      case 'header':
   134	        value = c.req.header()
   135	        break
   136	      case 'cookie':
   137	        value = getCookie(c)
   138	        break
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    const res = await validationFunc(value as never, c as never)
   142	
   143	    if (res instanceof Response) {
   144	      return res
   145	    }
   146	
   147	    c.req.addValidatedData(target, res as never)
   148	
   149	    await next()
   150	  }
   151	}

    98	  #getDecodedParam(key: string): string | undefined {
    99	    const paramKey = this.#matchResult[0][this.routeIndex][1][key]
   100	    const param = this.#getParamValue(paramKey)
   101	    return param ? (/\%/.test(param) ? tryDecodeURIComponent(param) : param) : undefined
   102	  }

   104	  #getAllDecodedParams(): Record<string, string> {
   105	    const decoded: Record<string, string> = {}
   106	
   107	    const keys = Object.keys(this.#matchResult[0][this.routeIndex][1])
   108	    for (const key of keys) {
   109	      const value = this.#getParamValue(this.#matchResult[0][this.routeIndex][1][key])
   110	      if (value && typeof value === 'string') {
   111	        decoded[key] = /\%/.test(value) ? tryDecodeURIComponent(value) : value
   112	      }
   113	    }

   212	  #cachedBody = (key: keyof Body) => {
   213	    const { bodyCache, raw } = this
   214	    const cachedBody = bodyCache[key]
   215	
   216	    if (cachedBody) {
   217	      return cachedBody
   218	    }
   219	
   220	    const anyCachedKey = Object.keys(bodyCache)[0]
   221	    if (anyCachedKey) {
   222	      return (bodyCache[anyCachedKey as keyof Body] as Promise<BodyInit>).then((body) => {
   223	        if (anyCachedKey === 'json') {
   224	          body = JSON.stringify(body)
   225	        }
   226	        return new Response(body)[key]()
   227	      })
   228	    }
   229	
   230	    return (bodyCache[key] = raw[key]())
   231	  }
